Note.— The population of New South Wales Includes 4,287 aborigines (full bloods and half-
castes in a nomadic state), of whom 2,451 were males and 1,836 females. Included in the figures
for Victoria are 271 full-blooded aborigines, 163 males, 108 females; in those for Queensland, 6,670
full-blooded and half-castes aborigines, 3,862 males, 2,808 females; and in those for Western Australia
951 half-caste aborigines, 492 males and 459 females.

Notf..— The figures in regard to shipping are exclusive of coastal trade. They are of little value
for comparative purposes, as the steamers trading between Australia and Europe usually call at the
principal port of Western Australia. South Australia, Victoria, and New South Wales, and are set
down in the local returns for the same voyage as twice entered and twice cleared from the ports of
the three States first-named, and also as entered and cleared from the ports of New South Wales.
